<p>The <b>1977 FIFA World Youth Championship</b> was the inaugural staging of the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="FIFA U-20 World Cup">FIFA World Youth Championship</a> and was held in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> from 27 June to 10 July 1977. The tournament took place in four venues — <a href="/wiki/Tunis" title="Tunis">Tunis</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rades" title="Rades">Rades</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sousse" title="Sousse">Sousse</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sfax" title="Sfax">Sfax</a> — where a total of 28 matches were played, the smallest number in its history. The winner was <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union_national_under-20_football_team" title="Soviet Union national under-20 football team">USSR</a>, who beat <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_under-20_football_team" title="Mexico national under-20 football team">Mexico</a> by a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout_(football)" title="Penalty shootout (football)">penalty shootout</a>, in a final held at Tunis's <a href="/wiki/Stade_El_Menzah" title="Stade El Menzah">Stade El Menzah</a>.</p>
<p>The Tournament Committee was chaired by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> Vice-President <a href="/wiki/Harry_Cavan" title="Harry Cavan">Harry Cavan</a>, who had spearheaded the creation of the World Youth Championship.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Squads">Squads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1977_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Squads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>For a list of all squads that played in the final tournament, see <i><a href="/wiki/1977_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship_squads" title="1977 FIFA World Youth Championship squads">1977 FIFA World Youth Championship squads</a></i>.</p>

<table class="wikitable" style="margin:auto; text-align:center">
<tr>
<th>Golden Shoe</th>
<th>Golden Ball</th>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Goalscorers">Goalscorers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1977_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Goalscorers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Guina of Brazil won the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-20_World_Cup#Golden_Shoe" title="FIFA U-20 World Cup">Golden Shoe</a> award for scoring four goals. In total, 70 goals were scored by 49 different players, with none of them credited as own goal.</p>
<dl>
<dt>4 goals</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil"><img alt="Brazil" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" width="22"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Aguinaldo_Roberto_Gallon" title="Aguinaldo Roberto Gallon">Guina</a></li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1977_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-FRA_v_ESP-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-FRA_v_ESP_1-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The official FIFA match report indicates that the first half finished 1:0 for France, but this contradicts the data on the scoring.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-Azim_Zade-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Azim_Zade_2-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The FIFA match report states "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_SFSR" title="Russian SFSR">Russia</a>" here, which is an <a href="/wiki/Anachronism" title="Anachronism">anachronism</a>.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-No_ref-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-No_ref_3-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-No_ref_3-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The official FIFA report accounts no minute for this goal.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-Gebreyesus-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Gebreyesus_4-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The FIFA match report anachronistically states <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a>.</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
